    <script type="text/javascript">
var iframeAuthSites = function(){
    //note this will only work when the page first loads in an iframe
	var path = document.referrer;
	if(path){
		if(path.indexOf("stumbleupon")!=-1){
			return true;
		}else if(path.indexOf("allmyfaves")!=-1){
			return true;
		}
	}
	return false;
};
if(window != top && iframeAuthSites()==false) {
	ele_body = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
	ele_body.className = ele_body.className + " iframe";
	bodyid = ele_body.id;
	if(bodyid=="home" || bodyid=="index_regwall"){
		var url = "http://" + window.location.hostname;
		if(window.location.port){
			url += ":" + window.location.port;
		}
		window.top.location.href = url + "/";
	}
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }
</script>

  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>

  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }

  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>

    <script type="text/javascript">
var iframeAuthSites = function(){
    //note this will only work when the page first loads in an iframe
	var path = document.referrer;
	if(path){
		if(path.indexOf("stumbleupon")!=-1){
			return true;
		}else if(path.indexOf("allmyfaves")!=-1){
			return true;
		}
	}
	return false;
};
if(window != top && iframeAuthSites()==false) {
	ele_body = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
	ele_body.className = ele_body.className + " iframe";
	bodyid = ele_body.id;
	if(bodyid=="home" || bodyid=="index_regwall"){
		var url = "http://" + window.location.hostname;
		if(window.location.port){
			url += ":" + window.location.port;
		}
		window.top.location.href = url + "/";
	}
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }
</script>

  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>

	bodyid = ele_body.id;
	if(bodyid=="home" || bodyid=="index_regwall"){
		var url = "http://" + window.location.hostname;
		if(window.location.port){
			url += ":" + window.location.port;
		}
		window.top.location.href = url + "/";
	}
}
</script>

<script type='text/javascript'>
  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }
</script>

  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>

  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }
</script>

  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>	
  	<div class="clear"></div>
	</div>

  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }

	<a class="close _sclose" href="#"><em></em></a>
  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>

var iframeAuthSites = function(){
    //note this will only work when the page first loads in an iframe
	var path = document.referrer;
	if(path){
		if(path.indexOf("stumbleupon")!=-1){
			return true;
		}else if(path.indexOf("allmyfaves")!=-1){
			return true;
		}
	}
	return false;
};
if(window != top && iframeAuthSites()==false) {
	ele_body = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
	ele_body.className = ele_body.className + " iframe";
	bodyid = ele_body.id;
	if(bodyid=="home" || bodyid=="index_regwall"){
		var url = "http://" + window.location.hostname;
		if(window.location.port){
			url += ":" + window.location.port;
		}
		window.top.location.href = url + "/";
	}
}

<script type='text/javascript'>
  function rememberChoice() {
    var cName = 'promo2done';
    var nDays= 180;
    var expire = new Date(new Date().getTime() + (3600000 * 24 * nDays));
    var cVal = cName + "=1;expires="+expire.toGMTString() + ";path=/;";
    document.cookie = cVal;
    $('#refer-banner').slideUp();
    return true;
  }
</script>

	<a class="close _sclose" href="#"><em></em></a>
  <div class="faq_container">
    <p class='title'>What is Foodily?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily is the world's largest social recipe network. With Foodily, it's easy to discover, collect and share the food you love. Add your own recipes and follow friends and experts to inspire you. 
    </p>

    <p class='title'>Why don't we show the instructions on some recipes?</p>
    <p class="line divider">Foodily respects the chefs, bloggers and cookbook authors that create many of the amazing recipes you find on Foodily. We're here to help you find the right recipe to meet your needs, but the actual recipe lives where it was created and that's where we send you to get preparation instructions. We realize it's an extra click for you, but we're pretty sure you'll agree the recipe instructions should stay with the recipe creator.</p>
  
  	<p class='title'>How do I use Foodily to search for recipes?</p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>dish type</span>............................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/dinner">dinner</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/appetizers">appetizers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search <span class='strong'>specific food sites</span>................................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/mario-batali-pasta">Mario Batali pasta</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/pioneer-woman-desserts">Pioneer Woman desserts</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span>Search by <span class='strong'>nutrition interest</span> or <span class='strong'>diet</span>...................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-carb-casseroles">low-carb casseroles</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/low-fat-picatta">low-fat picatta</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Include</span> any ingredients you want.......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/chicken-with-rosemary">chicken with rosemary</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/lemon-with-capers">lemon with capers</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider"><span class='bullet'>&raquo;</span><span class='strong'>Exclude</span> any ingredients you don't......................<span class='weak'>e.g. <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/breakfast-without-eggs">breakfast without eggs</a> or <a class="_fbapp_target" href="/s/cakes-without-chocolate">cakes without chocolate</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line">Or put them all together! <a class="_fbapp_target" href='/s/epicurious-vegetarian-healthy-pasta-with-tomato-without-basil'>Epicurious, vegetarian, healthy, pasta, with tomato, without basil</a></span></p>
  	<p class="line divider">Of course, if you have other ideas for how we can support the way you want to search - <a class="_fbapp_target" href='http://foodily.uservoice.com/forums/88631'>let us know.</a></p>
  	
  	<p class='title'>I'd like to delete my account. Can I do that? </p>
    <p class="line divider">Of course! We'll take care of that for you. Just send an email to help@foodily.com. Please make sure you either send it from the email associated with the account, or include the specific email for us to reference. We'll send you a confirmation email once we've deleted your account.</p>
